 agar bharat or pakistan ke aapasi sambandhon ko behatar banane kii koshish sachhee or gambhir he to hurriyat ke alaava, bharat ke najariye se kam se kam chaar aise moolbhoot masale hai, jinke hal kii jarurat he
 First, to find a solution to the Kashmir issue
 donon sarkarein un uplabdhiyon ko nakaarne ke mood main dikh rahi hai, jo janvari, 2004 main atal bihari vaajapeyi ke islamabad daure main islamabad ghoshnaptr jari hone, tathaa usee saal satinder lamba or tarik azeej ke bich back-door policy ke tahat baatcheet shuru hone ke baad ke teen saalon main hasil huin
 Documents show that the interlocutors had agreed that the final solution to the Jammu and Kashmir issue would be to avoid border and common people interchange, and that we should increase the movement of friends and relatives across the Line of Control
 Have to focus on
 kaarobaar or saanskrithik sambandhon ko kashmir ke donon hisson main badhaane par bhi sahmati jataai gai thi, or ek sanyukt prabandhan ke jariye line of control ke aar-paar rah rahe logon ke liye seemaa rekha ko apraasangik banane kii baat bhi shaamil thi
 It is true that this agreement achieved under the back-door policy was not brought before either of the governments for confirmation, but since the negotiators were talking as representatives of their respective governments, such It can be said that the talks give some idea about the government's proposals
 doosraa masalaa, line of control (or kai baar antarrashtriya seemaa rekha par) par golibari se judaa he, jo kai baar barbar jaan padataa he, jisamen na keval sena ke javaanon kii maut hoti he, balki seemaa ke aasapaas rahane vaale aam naagarik bhi isaki chapet main aa jate hai
 Their property is also damaged, and many times they have to be displaced
 aisi nindaneey ghatnaon se seemaa ke donon ore tanaav badhata he, jise media hawa detaa he
 The reality is that there is an 'inverse' relationship between talks and incidents of firing on the border
 varsh 2004 se 2008 ke bich seemapar se golibari kii ghatnaon or usase hone vaali mauton ke maamalon main kami dekhne ko mili, jab usee dauraan donon mulkon ke bich baatcheet jari thi
 After the 26 / 11 incident, as the negotiation process stopped, the number of cross-border firing cases increased in severity
 so, agar uddeshy gairzaruri jaani nuksaan ko rokna, sampatti kii barbaadi ko rokna, or seemaa se sate logon kaa visthaapan rokna he, to hamen samajhnaa hoga ki baatcheet kii prakriya shuru hone se tanaav kam hota he
 This will prevent all other unfortunate incidents, but if we do not talk, the lives of common people will be at stake
 teesraa masalaa, pakistan dwaara islamabad ghoshnaptr (2004) main kiye gaye seemapar se aatankwaad rokane or aisi ghatnaon ke doshiyon ko dandit karne ke vaadon se judaa he
 The question arises as to what action Pakistan has taken to prevent terrorism from across the border and to punish those who commit such heinous incidents
 haalanki pakistan ko kathghare main khadaa karnaa, baatcheet kii prakriya ko shuru karne ke lihaaj se uchit nahin he, haalanki nisandeh pakistan khud hi iske liye jimmedaar he
 India can remind Pakistan of its commitment in this matter only through dialogue
 pakistan kii sarazamin se aatankwaad kaa khatm hona baatcheet shuru karne kii shart honi chahie yaa phir baatcheet kaa masalaa hona chahie
 
 
 The Not only this, terrorist acts are also carried out by Indians in many parts of India, so should India have sympathy for Pakistan, because it is the most terrorism affected country in the world
 aatankwaad kii vajah se, or pakistani jameen par, khaskar uttar-pashchimi pakistan main aatankwaad ke khilaaf paak-america yuddh ke chalate ab tak 40 hajaar pakistaniyon kii maut ho chuki he
 Should India not notice that terrorists have heavily targeted Pakistan's government establishments, including ISI headquarters in Lahore, army headquarters in Rawalpindi and Mehran Naval Center on the outskirts of Karachi
 kya bharat or pakistan aapas main, or saarc ke fremawork main bhi aapasi sambandhon ko behatar nahin bana sakate, taaki aatankwaad se nipatane ke liye donon desh ek behatar manch bana saken
 The fourth issue is a confusing question with whom to talk in Pakistan
 bharat main lagaataar yah tark diya jaataa he ki pakistan main loktantr behad kamjor he, haalanki aisa he nahin, lekin sarkaar, sena, khufia samudaay, shaktishaalee dharmik guru or bandook liye jehadi, inamen se pakistan main faisla koun letaa he
 
 
 The Whom should we talk to? 
 
 ? unase baatcheet karne kaa kya phayda, jinke haath main vastav main takat nahin hai
 
 
 The We must admit that Pakistan is a sovereign country, so it is not possible to negotiate with anyone other than the government, and at the same time it has to be kept in mind that India has been interacting with the government channels - and often they were successful
 is
 duusare saajheedaaron ko baatcheet main shaamil karnaa jamini sachai ko pahchaan lenaa bhale hi ho saktaa he, lekin yah ek chuni hui sarkaar ke bharat se baatcheet nahin karne kaa aadhaar nahin ho saktaa
 For example, can the Indian government allow Pakistani negotiators to talk directly to the Indian Army Chief, as the Indian Armed Forces are reluctant to leave Siachen
 pakistan kii chuni hui sarkaar ko sabhi gharelu sanghathanon kaa dhyaan rakhana hoga, or aisa hi bharat ko bhi karnaa hoga
 But democratically elected government has to be seen as a toy in the hands of non-power partners, undermining Pakistan's democracy, which India has always believed to be very important for improving india-pakistan relations
 is tarah, tamaam pakshon ko dekhte hue bhavishya ke liye do vikalp najar aate hai
 First, we should ignore Pakistan (whether benign or hick-ridden)
 bharat main bauddhik chintakon kaa ek tabaka (shaayad pakistan main bhi) yah maanata he ki kisi bhi ahm mudde par koi pragati nahin ho sakati he, isliye budhimaani pakistan kii upeksha karne main he or hamen videsh niti ke duusare aayam ko praathamikta deni chahie
 But adopting this option would mean accepting all issues with Pakistan
 lekin kya bharat line of control par golibari kii upeksha kar saktaa he
 
 
 The Can Pakistan ignore the lack of water in the Indus River? 
 
 ? kya bharat seemapar se ghuspaith kii upeksha kar saktaa he
 
 
 The Can Pakistan turn a blind eye to smuggling from across the border? 
 
 ? kya bharat seemapar se aane vaale aatankwaadiyon kii upeksha kar saktaa he
 
 
 The Can Pakistan give up its claim on Kashmir without final agreement
 
 
 ? kya pakistan siachin, sarkreek or wooler-tulbul par apane daavon ko anishchiya main chhod saktaa he
 
 
 The Can we leave the transit route reaching Afghanistan via Pakistan
 
 
 ? kya donon main se koi bhi desh ek-duusare ke saath kaarobaar ke avasaron ko ganvaa saktaa he
 
 
 The Will the world let the matter go like this
 
 
 ? kya hamaari parmaanu kshamtaaon se duniya bhar main chintaa nahin badhegi
 
 
 The Therefore, no, mutual neglect is not an option
 yah zyaada se zyaada ek sanak ho sakati he
 Whether we like it or not, Pakistan will continue to hurt us, and we will do the same with Pakistan, not only politically, but also in everyday life on both sides of the border, whether it is about the issue of divided families, about Bollywood
 Of shared love
 aise main agar, paraspar upeksha or paraspar sahmati kii sambhaavnaaen khaarij ho jaati hai to aage badhane kaa rasta kya bachataa he
 
 
 The Currently, there is only one option
 vah he bharat or pakistan ke bich baatcheet, jo abhi thande baste main chali gai he, lekin baatcheet ke teble par lautne ke bare main baatcheet shuru honi chahie
 Such efforts can be made at the diplomatic level, or even through a covert back-door channel, so that when the tension is reduced and efforts are made to improve mutual relations, negotiations can begin
 ise aap nirbaadh or baadhit nahin hone vaali prakriya ke taur bhi dekh sakate hai
